msg:During the Chinese New Year, the school requires children not to leave Shanghai, so they can only take her to play in the city. Because the little guy wanted to go to the safari park, but he didn't want to go home directly, so he chose Powerlong Radisson. On the day of check-in on the fifth day of the new year, the hotel gave me a free room type upgrade, and upgraded the executive suite I booked to a presidential suite ! The presidential suite is really big. There are ovens and induction cookers. If you don't want to go out and just stay in the hotel, you can make delicious food yourself. After entering the presidential suite, there is a hall on the right hand side, which is divided into a living room and a dining room. There is a TV wall in the middle of the two halls as a separation. There is also a small office and study room in the hall. On the left side of the suite entrance is the bedroom area. The bedroom faces east, and when the weather is good, you can watch the sunrise (please ignore my photography skills in Figure 9). The bathroom in the bedroom is very large, with floor-to-ceiling windows facing east. When the sun is shining, open the electric curtains and the whole bathroom is very comfortable. bright. There is a corridor from the bedroom to the living room. I like this, because those who play games in the living room will not disturb those who rest in the bedroom, which is very good. There is also a small bathroom on the right side of the suite entrance, which is convenient for watching TV and playing in the living room and eating in the dining room. There are not many varieties of breakfast in the hotel, but you can eat enough and basic nutrition can be guaranteed. The hotel is still far from the Caolu Baolong City Plaza on the edge, and it takes about ten minutes to walk there. The hotel staff are very good, the front desk is warmly received, and the staff will take the initiative to say hello when they encounter the staff in the aisle on the floor. Stayed for three days and two nights and felt good all day.
